<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 1; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(1);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__PRMyRequisitionDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__PRMyRequisitionDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PRMyRequisitionDataView', GridHeight: '400', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__PRMyRequisitionDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__PRMyRequisitionDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '400', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__PRMyRequisitionDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__PRMyRequisitionDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'PRMyRequisitionDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'PRMyRequisitionDataView', GridHeight: '400', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PRMyRequisitionDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divPRMyRequisitionDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___PRMyRequisitionDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'PRMyRequisitionDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PRMyRequisitionDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PRMyRequisitionDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("PRMyRequisitionDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___PRMyRequisitionDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("PRMyRequisitionDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__PRMyRequisitionDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__PRMyRequisitionDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__PRMyRequisitionDataView() {
        var gridName = 'PRMyRequisitionDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___PRMyRequisitionDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_PRMyRequisitionDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "PRMyRequisitionDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_PRMyRequisitionDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__PRMyRequisitionDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__PRMyRequisitionDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divPRMyRequisitionDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

    var _lastStatusType = 1;
    function onLinkClick(statusType) {
        _lastStatusType = statusType;

        $("#lnkActiveLink").removeClass();
        $("#lnkIssuedLink").removeClass();
        $("#lnkAllLink").removeClass();

        if (statusType == 1) {
            $('#lnkActiveLink').addClass('ActiveLink');
            $('#lnkIssuedLink').addClass('NormalLink');
            $('#lnkAllLink').addClass('NormalLink');
        }
        else if (statusType == 2) {
            $('#lnkActiveLink').addClass('NormalLink');
            $('#lnkIssuedLink').addClass('ActiveLink');
            $('#lnkAllLink').addClass('NormalLink');
        }
        else if (statusType == 3) {
            $('#lnkActiveLink').addClass('NormalLink');
            $('#lnkIssuedLink').addClass('NormalLink');
            $('#lnkAllLink').addClass('ActiveLink');
        }

        ShowRequisitions(statusType);
    }

    function GotoPurchaseOrder(poNumber) {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/PurchaseRequisitionGoToSource',
            cache: false,
            data: { purchaseorderNumber: poNumber },
            type: 'GET',

            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {

                    if (result.Success === true) {
                        if (result.IsTargetPopup) {
                            ShowPODetailPopup(result.Url, result.TargetPopupTitle);

                        }
                        else {
                            window.location.href = result.Url;
                        }
                    }
                    else {

                        gotoSourceInProgress = false;
                        ShowOkDialog('Purchase Order', 'Purchase order not found');
                    }
                }
            }

        });
    }

    function ShowRequisitions(statusType) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/GetMyRequisition",
            data: { statusType: statusType },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    grid.dataSource.read();
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {

        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "PurchaseRequisitionView");

        $('#lnkActiveLink').addClass('NormalLink');
        $('#lnkIssuedLink').addClass('NormalLink');
        $('#lnkAllLink').addClass('ActiveLink');

        onLinkClick(3);
        var openPopup = $("#FromPopup").val();
        var prId = $("#PRId").val();
        
        if (openPopup == "True") {
            var PRMyRequisitionDataView = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            PRMyRequisitionDataView.dataSource.bind("change", function () {
                if (PRMyRequisitionDataView.dataSource.data().length &gt; 0) {
                    PRMyRequisitionDataView.dataSource.unbind("change");
                    var grid = $("#divPRMyRequisitionDataView").data("AptaDataView");
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow(prId, aptaDataViewSelection);                    
                }
            });

        }
    });

            ResizeGridForAutoHeight("#PRMyRequisitionDataView");
        }
    }

    $("#btnAdd__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var id = "|3"
        var data, options;

        data = { Id: id, origin: 2 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/CreateMyRequisitionPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowRequisition")
            .SetIsModal(true)
            .SetContent(options)
            .SetWidth(1000)
            .SetHeight("90%")
            .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
            .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionScreen)
            .SetTitle('Add Purchase Requisition');
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionView", null);
    });

    $("#btnEdit__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function (e) {

            EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
        }
    });

    function EditPurchaseRequisitionFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data, options;

        data = { Id: id, origin: 2, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: -1 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowRequisition")
       .SetIsModal(true)
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetWidth(1000)
       .SetHeight("90%")
       .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionScreen)
       .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
       .SetTitle('Edit Purchase Requisition')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionView", null);
    }

    function ReturnFromRequisitionScreen() {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "PurchaseRequisitionView");
    }


    function ReturnFromRequisition() {
        var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }


    $('#btnEditAll__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (selectedRowId !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__PRMyRequisitionDataView').click();
        }
        $('#btnEdit__PurchaseRequisitionView').click();
    });



    $("#btnEdit__PurchaseRequisitionView_Popup").click(function (e) {

        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }

        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
            var passValue = selectedRowIds.split(',');
            window.location.href = "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/MyDetails?Id=" + passValue[0] + "&amp;statusType=" + -1 + "&amp;ReturnScreen=MyPR";
        }
    });

    function RefreshOnDeleteRequisitions(selectedRowId) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divPRMyRequisitionDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/MultipleDelete',
                 { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRowIds: selectedRowId },
                'MyPurchaseRequisition', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function DeleteRequisitions() {
        var dataView = 'PRMyRequisitionDataView';

        var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteRequisitions(selectedRowId); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    $("#btnDelete__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function (e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        if (ValidateGridSelection("PRMyRequisitionDataView", true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected requisitions?", DeleteRequisitions);
        }

    });

    $('#btnWithdraw_PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function () {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var selectedRowId = GetGridSelectedId('PRMyRequisitionDataView');

        if (!OnlyOneItemSelected(selectedRowId)) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Withdraw", "Are you sure you would like to withdraw this requisition?", function () { Withdrawn(selectedRowId) });
    });

    function Withdrawn(prId) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/WithdrawRequisition",
            data: { prId: prId },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    grid.dataSource.read();
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    var submitForAllNo = false;
    var submitForAllYes = false;
    $("#btnSubmitRequisition__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        submitForAllNo = false;
        submitForAllYes = false;

        if (!$("#divPRMyRequisitionDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        ShowYesNoDialog('Confirm Submit', 'Are you sure you want to submit the selected requisition(s)?', function () {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition("-1", false, false, 'MyPurchaseRequisition'); });
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
        });

    });

    function RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(requisitionId, overbudget, moveNext, key) {
        var operationResultId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divPRMyRequisitionDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/SubmitMassRequsition',
                     { requisitionId: requisitionId, overBudget: overbudget, moveNext: moveNext, operationResultId: operationResultId, key: key },
                key, function (result) {
                    if (result.Success == 1) {
                        RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key);

                    } else if (result.Success == 3) {

                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key);
                        }
                        else {

                            if ('False' == 'True') {
                                result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Do you wish to continue?"
                                ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("My Purchase Requisitions", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, true, false, key); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, true, key); submitForAllNo = e; });
                            }
                            else {
                                // create an appropriate error message
                                result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Purchase Request cannot be submitted."
                                ShowOkDialog("My Purchase Requisitions", result.Message, null);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    else if (result.Success == 4) {

                        //4 indicates process end,
                        submitForAllNo = false;
                        submitForAllYes = false;
                        var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        ShowResultGrid();
                    }
                    else {
                        RefreshOnSubmitMassRequisition(result.InvoiceId, false, false, key);

                    }
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults", false);
    }

    function ShowResultGrid()
    {
        ShowMassActionResultsPopup('popupwindowMassActionResults');
    }

    $("#btnAttachments__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function () {

        if (ValidateGridSelection("PRMyRequisitionDataView", false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) {
            var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("PRMyRequisitionDataView");
            NavigateTo("/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/PRAttachments" + "/" + selectedRowIds);
        }

    });

    $("#btnCopyRequisition__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function () {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (ValidateGridSelection("PRMyRequisitionDataView", false, "Selection", "Please select a single record to perform this operation.")) {

            var data = "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds;
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/CopyRequisition",
                data: data,
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result == "") {
                        ReturnFromAction();
                        ShowAjaxMessage("Purchase Requisition copied successfully.", "success");
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                    }
                    //ResizeGridOnMessage(true);
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                }
            });
        }
    });

    function ReturnFromAction() {
        var grid = $("#PRMyRequisitionDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }

    $("#btnPrint__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function () {

                    .SetIsModal(true)
                    .SetTitle('Print Purchase Requisition').SetWidth(650).SetHeight(150);
    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    });

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }

<script>
    var PRloadTabRequestedItems = true;
    var PRloadTabApprovalHistory = true;
    var PRloadTabAttachmentView = true;

	function onActivate(e) {
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        var activeTabStripText = $("#tabstripPR").data("FINSUITabStrip").GetActiveTabText()
        if (activeTabStripText == 'Requested Items') {
			if (PRloadTabRequestedItems) {
				if (PRloadTabRequestedItems &amp;&amp; '0' &gt; 0) {
                    LoadGridOnDemand__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView();
					PRloadTabRequestedItems = false;
                }
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");
        }

        else if (activeTabStripText == 'Approval History') {
            if (PRloadTabApprovalHistory) {
                var grid = $("#ApprovalTransactionsDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                grid.dataSource.read();
                PRloadTabApprovalHistory = false;
            }
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", null);
        }

        else if (activeTabStripText == 'Attached Files') {
            if (PRloadTabAttachmentView) {
				LoadGridOnDemand__AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3();
				var grid = $("#AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3").data("kendoGrid");
                grid.dataSource.read();
                PRloadTabAttachmentView = false;
            }
			ResizeGridForAutoHeight("#AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3")
			RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3__PurchaseRequisition", "AttachmentFrameworkDataViewLevel3__PurchaseRequisition");
        }

    }

    $("#btnCancel__PurchaseRequisitionView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        closRequisitioneWindow(e);

    });

    function closRequisitioneWindow(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var grid = $("#"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
        if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
    }

    function OnRequisitionerChange() {
        if (0 ==  0) {
            RefreshShipToList();
        }
    }

    function RefreshShipToList() {
                $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/RefreshShipToList',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: { requisitionerID: $("#RequisitionerId").data("kendoComboBox").value() },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result !== null &amp;&amp; result.responseText != "0") {
                    $("#DestinationId").data("kendoComboBox").value(result.responseText);
                }
                else {
                    $("#DestinationId").data("kendoComboBox").value('');
                }
            },
            error: function (result) {
            }
            });
    }

    function OnChange_PRType() {
        OnPRTypeChage(false);
    }

    function OnPRTypeChage(init) {
        $("#WarehouseId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(false);
        $("#SuggestedOrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(true);
        var approvaltype = $("#PRType").data("kendoComboBox").value();
        if (approvaltype != null) {
            if (approvaltype === 'L') {
                approvaltype = 4;
                var combobox = $("#WarehouseId").data("kendoComboBox");
                if (combobox.dataSource._data.length == 1) {
                    combobox.select(0);
                }
                $("#WarehouseId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(true);
            }
            else if (approvaltype === 'W') {
                approvaltype = 5;
                var combobox = $("#WarehouseId").data("kendoComboBox");
                if (combobox.dataSource._data.length == 1) {
                    combobox.select(0);
                }
                $("#WarehouseId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(true);
                $("#SuggestedOrderingVendorId").data("FINSComboBox").SetVisible(false);
            }
            else {
                approvaltype = 3;
            }
        }

        if ('My Purchase Requisitions' === 'Admin Purchase Requisitions') {
            $.ajax({
                url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/RefreshApproverListPopup',
                cache: false,
                dataType: 'JSON',
                data: { approvalType: approvaltype },
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result !== null) {

                        var dropDown = $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox");
                        if (dropDown != null) {
                            dropDown.dataSource.data(result);
                            dropDown.refresh();
                            var len = dropDown.dataSource.data().length;
                            if (len &gt;= 1) {
                                dropDown.value('');
                            }
                            else {
                                dropDown.value('');
                            }
                        }

                        OnSelectedIndexChangePopup_ApproverListComboBox();
                    }
                },
                error: function (result) {
                }
            });
        }
        else if (init == false) {
            ReloadRequisitioner('');
        }
    }

    function OnSelectedIndexChangePopup_ApproverListComboBox() {
        var approverId = null;

        var dropDown = $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox");
        if (dropDown != null) {
            let tempApproverId = dropDown.value();
            if (tempApproverId != null) {
                let tempArray = tempApproverId.split("~");
                if (tempArray.length &gt; 0) {
                    approverId = tempArray[0];
                }
            }
        }
        ReloadRequisitioner(approverId);
    }

    function ReloadRequisitioner(approver) {
        let cbRqn = $("#RequisitionerId").data("FINSComboBox");
        if (cbRqn != null) {
            let showAllRequisitioners = false;
            let chk = $("#ShowAllRequisitioners");
            if (chk != null) {
                showAllRequisitioners = chk.prop('checked') ? true : false;
            }
            cbRqn.DataParameters.ShowAllRequisitioners = showAllRequisitioners;
            cbRqn.DataParameters.ApproverId = approver;

            var approvaltype = $("#PRType").data("kendoComboBox").value();
            if (approvaltype === 'L') {
                cbRqn.DataParameters.RequisitionerType = 'ReplenishmentRequisition';
            }
            else if (approvaltype === 'W') {
                cbRqn.DataParameters.RequisitionerType = 'WarehouseRequisition';
            }
            else {
                cbRqn.DataParameters.RequisitionerType = 'PurchaseRequisition';
            }

            cbRqn.ReloadData();
            if (cbRqn.Value != null &amp;&amp; !cbRqn.DoesValueExistInSource(cbRqn.Value)) {
                cbRqn.SetValue("");
            }
            if (showAllRequisitioners || approver) { cbRqn.SetValue(""); }
        }
    }

    function OnCheckChange_ApproverList() {
        OnSelectedIndexChangePopup_ApproverListComboBox();
    }

    function OnCheckChange_AllRequisitions() {
        var isChecked = $('#ShowAllRequisitioners').prop('checked') ? true : false;

        if (isChecked) {
            $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox").enable(false);
            ReloadRequisitioner('');
        }
        else {
            $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox").enable();
            OnSelectedIndexChangePopup_ApproverListComboBox();
        }
    }

    function ProcessCartItems(cartID) {
        var prID = '0';
        NavigateTo('ProcessPunchoutMessage' + "?cartId=" + cartID + "&amp;prID=" + prID + "&amp;statusType=" + '3');
    }

    function DontProcessCartItems(cartID) {
        var prID = '0';
        var data = { prID: prID, cartId: cartID };

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/DontProcessCart',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result !== "") {

                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function GotoPurchaseOrder(poNumber) {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/PurchaseRequisitionGoToSource',
            cache: false,
            data: { purchaseorderNumber: poNumber },
            type: 'GET',

            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {

                    if (result.Success === true) {
                        if (result.IsTargetPopup) {
                            OpenPODetailPopupfromPR(result.Url, result.TargetPopupTitle);

                        }
                        else {
                            window.location.href = result.Url;
                        }
                    }
                    else {

                        gotoSourceInProgress = false;
                        ShowOkDialog('Purchase Order', 'Purchase order not found');
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function ResizeGridOnMessage(doReSize) {
        if ('My Purchase Requisitions' === 'Admin Purchase Requisitions') {
            NavigateTo('' + "?Id=" + '0' + "&amp;statusType=" + '3');
        }
        else {
            NavigateTo('' + "?Id=" + '0' + "&amp;statusType=" + '3' + "&amp;returnScreen=" + 'MyPR');
        }
    }
</script>

<script>

    $('#btnSaveAndSubmit__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        ShowYesNoDialog('Confirm Submit', 'Are you sure you would like to submit the selected requisition?', function () {
            SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "Submit")
        });

    });

    function SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, operation) {
        $("#PROperation").val(0);
        $("#PRIsSubmit").val(true);
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
        var destinationID = $("#DestinationId").val();

        var rName;
        var requisitionerId;
        var validationMessage = '';

        if ('0' &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; ('My Purchase Requisitions' == 'Admin Purchase Requisitions' || 'My Purchase Requisitions' == 'My Purchase Requisition Approvals')) {
            rName = $('#RequestorName').val();
            requisitionerId = '';
            $("#RequestorName").data("FINSUITextInput").SetValue(rName);
            $('#RequisitionerId').val(requisitionerId);
        }
        else {
            rName = $('#RequisitionerId').data("kendoComboBox").text();
            requisitionerId = $('#RequisitionerId').data("kendoComboBox").value();
            $("#RequisitionerId").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(requisitionerId);
            $('#RequestorName').val(rName);
        }

        if (typeof destinationID == 'undefined' || destinationID == '')
            validationMessage += 'Ship To is required' + '&lt;br /&gt;';
        if (typeof requisitionerId == 'undefined' || requisitionerId == '')
            validationMessage += 'Requisitioner Name is required.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';

        if (validationMessage != '') {

            ShowAjaxMessage(validationMessage, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        var form = $("#RequisitionDetails");
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: form.attr('action'),
            data: form.serialize(),
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == true) {

                    if (operation == "Submit")
                    {
                        SubmitRequisitions(false, e);
                    }

                    else if (operation == "Approve")
                    {
                        ApproveRequisitionOnPopup(e);
                    }

                    else if (operation == "Disapprove")
                    {
                        RefreshPopupAfterDisapproveRequisition(e);
                    }

                    else if (operation == "CopyRequisition")
                    {
                        CopyRequisitionPopup(e);
                    }

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

    function SubmitRequisitions(overBudget, e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
        var data = { overBudget: overBudget, requisitionId: '0' };
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/SubmitRequisition",
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {

                if (result.success == true) {
                    var navigationID = 0;

                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
                        navigationID = '0';
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                    }
                    var aptaDataViewSelection;
                    var grid = $("#"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                    if(grid != null)
                    {
                        aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    }
                    else{
                        aptaDataViewSelection = null;
                    }

                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
                else if (result.success == false) {
                    if ('False' == 'True') {
                        result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Do you wish to continue?"
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Purchase Requisition", result.Message, function () { SubmitRequisitions(true, e); });
                    }
                    else {
                        result.Message += "&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Purchase Requisition cannot be submitted."
                        ShowOkDialog("Purchase Requisition", result.Message, null);
                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            },
            error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnSave__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#PROperation").val(0);
        PurchaseRequisitionSave(false, false, e);
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").SetTitle('Edit Purchase Requisition');
    });

    $('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#PROperation").val(1);
        PurchaseRequisitionSave(true, false, e);
    });

    $('#btnSaveAndAdd__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").SetTitle('Add Purchase Requisition')
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#PROperation").val(2);
        PurchaseRequisitionSave(false, true, e);
    });

    $('#btnPrintMyPR__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowPrintPRs")
                    .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/PrintPurchaseRequisitionPrintSetup?" + "PRIdList=" + '0' + "&amp;dataView=None" + "&amp;PrintRequisitionPopup=" + 'MyPurchaseRequisition__PrintPurchaseRequisitionPrintSetup' })
                    .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionItem)
                    .SetTitle('Print Purchase Requisition').SetWidth(650).SetHeight(150);
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PrintPurchaseRequisition", null);

    });

    $('#btnApplyTax__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {

        data = { selectedRecords: '0', ApplyTaxPopup: 'MyPurchaseRequisition__ApplyTaxPopup' };

    });

    $('#btnAddShippingCost__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {

    $('#btnViewBudget__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var prItemID = '0';
        var data = { prId: '0' };
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/GetViewBudgetData",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result == "success") {
                    var url;
                    url = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/ViewBudgetPopup" };

                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupViewBudget")
                     .SetIsModal(true)
                     .SetContent(url)
                     .SetWidth(800)
                     .SetHeight(380)
                     .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                    .SetTitle('View Budget')
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
                    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "ViewBudgetPurchaseRequisition", null);
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error");
                }
            }
        });

    });

    function PurchaseRequisitionSave(saveNext, saveAdd, e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
        var destinationID = $("#DestinationId").val();

        var rName;
        var requisitionerId;
        var validationMessage = '';

        if ('0' &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; ('My Purchase Requisitions' == 'Admin Purchase Requisitions' || 'My Purchase Requisitions' == 'My Purchase Requisition Approvals')) {
            rName = $('#RequestorName').val();
            requisitionerId = '';
            $("#RequestorName").data("FINSUITextInput").SetValue(rName);
            $('#RequisitionerId').val(requisitionerId);
        }
        else {
            rName = $('#RequisitionerId').data("kendoComboBox").text();
            requisitionerId = $('#RequisitionerId').data("kendoComboBox").value();
            $("#RequisitionerId").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(requisitionerId);
            $('#RequestorName').val(rName);
        }

        if (typeof destinationID == 'undefined' || destinationID == '')
            validationMessage += 'Ship To is required' + '&lt;br /&gt;';
        if (typeof requisitionerId == 'undefined' || requisitionerId == '')
            validationMessage += 'Requisitioner Name is required.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';

        if (validationMessage != '') {

            ShowAjaxMessage(validationMessage, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        var form = $("#RequisitionDetails");
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: form.attr('action'),
            data: form.serialize(),
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == true) {

                    if (saveNext) {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div" + 'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup", data: { Id: '', origin: 'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' } });
                        var grid = $("#" + 'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();

                    }
                    else if (saveAdd) {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

                        var approverId = null;
                        var id = "";

                        if ('My Purchase Requisitions' == 'My Purchase Requisitions') {
                            id = "|3";
                        }
                        else {
                            id = '' + "|" + '3';
                        }

                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/CreateMyRequisitionPopup", data: { Id: id, origin: 'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' } });
                        var grid = $("#" + 'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }

                    else if ('0' &gt; 0) {
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
                        var grid = $("#" + 'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if (grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined) {
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        }
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    }
                    else {
                        var Id = result.Id;

                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div" + 'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup", data: { Id: Id, origin: 'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION', statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' }, type: "POST" });

                        var grid = $("#" + 'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if (grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined) {
                            grid.dataSource.read();
                        }
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();

                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });

    }

    $(document).ready(function () {

        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");

        var ctlSubmit = null;
        ctlSubmit = $("#btnSaveAndSubmit__PurchaseRequisitionView");
        if (ctlSubmit) {
            attachFINSTooltipToElement("btnSaveAndSubmit__PurchaseRequisitionView", 'Save And Submit Requisition');
        }
        var prID = '0';
        var prStatus = '';

        if (prID !== '0') {
            if ('False' == 'True' &amp;&amp; 'False' == 'False') {
                var data = { prID: prID };

                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    async: false,
                    url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/IsCartProcessed',
                    cache: false,
                    dataType: 'JSON',
                    data: data,
                    success: function (result) {
                        if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                            if (result !== "") {
                                if (result.Success) {
                                    ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Process Item", "A cart associated with this Purchase Request was not processed fully.  Would you like to add the " + result.ItemCount + " item(s) in this cart to the current Purchase Requests?", function () { ProcessCartItems(result.CartID) }, function () { DontProcessCartItems(result.CartID) });
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }

        var combobox = $("#PRType").data("FINSComboBox");

        if (prID !== '0') {

            if (prStatus != 'N') {
                combobox.SetReadOnly(true);
            }

            if ('My Purchase Requisitions' === 'Admin Purchase Requisitions') {
                $("#approverRequisition").hide();
            }
        }

        $("#ShowAllRequisitioners").change(OnCheckChange_AllRequisitions);
        var chk = $("#ShowAllRequisitioners");
        if (typeof chk == "undefined" || chk.length == 0) {

            var dropDown = $("#ApproverId").data("kendoComboBox");
            if (dropDown != null) {
                $("#ApproverId").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
            }
        }

        $("#PRType").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue('R');

        OnPRTypeChage(true);

        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        if ('My Purchase Requisitions' === 'My Purchase Requisition Approvals') {
            if ('False' === 'True' &amp;&amp; '0' &gt; 0) {
                ShowAjaxMessage('This requisition has been changed since you first opened it. The data on the screen has been updated. Please review and approve.', "notice");
            }
        }

    });

    $("#btnApplyAccountCode__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        if (!$("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        var data, options;

        data = { prId: '0', ApplyCodeToPRPopup: 'MyPurchaseRequisition__ApplyCodeToPRPopup' };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/ApplyCodeToPRPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowApplyCode")
         .SetIsModal(true)
         .SetContent(options)
         .SetWidth(650)
         .SetHeight(130)
         .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
        .SetTitle('Apply Account Codes to Requisition Items')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "ApplyAccountToPurchaseRequisition", null);

    });

    $("#btnDelete__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        if (!$("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you would like to delete the selected requisition item?", DeleteItemRequisitions);
    });

    function RefreshOnDeleteItemRequisitions(PRId) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var key = '';
        $("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/DeleteItemDetailsPopup',
                         { MassOperationId: massOperationId, PRId: PRId },
                    key, function (result) {
                        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                    }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function GetPurchaseRequsitionTotalAmount() {
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/GetPurchaseRequsitionTotalAmount",
            data: { prId: '0' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result !== null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    var tot = parseFloat(result.TotalAmount);
                    tot = tot.toFixed(2);
                    $("#RequisitionTotalAmount").text("$" + tot);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function DeleteItemRequisitions() {
        var prID = '0';

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/MassActionResults" }).SetonDeactivate(function () { GetPurchaseRequsitionTotalAmount(); }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteItemRequisitions(prID); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    }

    $("#btnShopOnline__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function () {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        var prID = '0';
        var vendorID = '';
        var data = { vendorID: vendorID };
        showSpinner();
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/IsEcommerceVendor',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result !== "")
                        if (result) {

                            NavigateTo("/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/RedirectToVendor" + "?PRId=" + prID + "&amp;vendorID=" + vendorID + "&amp;ecommerceAction=" + 'edit' + "&amp;statusType=" + '3'+ "&amp;fromPopup=true");
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowAjaxMessage("Vendor is not an eCommerce Vendor", "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                        }
                }
            }
        });
    });

    $("#btnAdd__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var ecommerce = 'False';
        var prID = '0';
        var vendorID = '';
        var data = { vendorID: vendorID };
        var openPRItemPopupAddMode = false;

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: '/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/IsEcommerceVendor',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result !== "")
                        if (result) {
                            NavigateTo("/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/RedirectToVendor" + "?PRId=" + prID + "&amp;vendorID=" + vendorID + "&amp;ecommerceAction=" + 'create' + "&amp;statusType=" + '3');
                        }
                        else {
                            openPRItemPopupAddMode = true;
                        }
                }
            }
        });
        if (openPRItemPopupAddMode == true) OpenPRItemPopupAddMode()
    });

    function OpenPRItemPopupAddMode()
    {
        var data, options;

        data = { Id: '0', statusType: '3', originPRItem: 'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/CreatePRItemPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowItemDetailsPopup")
            .SetIsModal(true)
            .SetContent(options)
            .SetHeight(500)
            .SetWidth(820)
            .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionItem)
            .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
            .SetTitle("Add Purchase Requisition Line Item");
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView", null);
    }

    $('#btnEditAll__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if (grid.dataSource.data().length &lt;= 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "There are currently no items in the list to Edit.", null);
            return;
        }
        var selectedRowId = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
        if (selectedRowId !== "-1") {
            $('.selectAll__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').click();
        }
        $('#btnEdit__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView').click();
    });

    $("#btnEdit__PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").click(function (e) {

        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#divPurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
            var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            EditPurchaseRequisitionItemFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
        }
    });

    function ItemDetails(Id) {
        EditPurchaseRequisitionItemFinsWindow(Id, null)
    }

    function EditPurchaseRequisitionItemFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data, options;

        data = { PRId: '0', prItemSequence: id, statusType: '3', originPRItem: 'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION', aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/ItemDetailsPopup", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupWindowItemDetailsPopup")
   .SetIsModal(true)
   .SetContent(options)
   .SetHeight(500)
   .SetWidth(820)
   .SetonClose(ReturnFromRequisitionItem)
   .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
   .SetTitle("Edit Purchase Requisition Line Item");
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView", null);
    }

    function ReturnFromRequisitionItem() {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys("PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup", "PurchaseRequisitionView", "PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView");
        var grid = $("#PurchaseRequisitionItemDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        if(grid != null)
            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
    }

    $('#btnCopy__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = '';

        if (prStatus != 'N' &amp;&amp; prStatus != 'R' &amp;&amp; prStatus != 'S') {
            CopyRequisitionPopup(e);
        }
        else
        {
            if (prStatus == 'S' &amp;&amp; 'My Purchase Requisitions' == 'My Purchase Requisitions') {
                CopyRequisitionPopup(e);
            }
            else{
                SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "CopyRequisition")
            }
        }
    });

    function CopyRequisitionPopup(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/CopyRequisitionPopup",
            data: { prId: '0' },
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {

                        var newPRID = result.NewPRID;
                        if (newPRID != null)
                        {
                            var aptaDataViewSelection;
                            var grid = $("#"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                            if(grid != null)
                            {
                                aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            }
                            else{
                                aptaDataViewSelection = null;
                            }

                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : newPRID, origin:'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3' },type:"POST"});
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

                        if(grid != null)
                            ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                    }

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnUndoSubmit__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Undo Submit", "Are you sure you would like to undo submit and change the requisition status back to New?", function () { UndoSubmiRequisitionPopup(e) });
    });

    function UndoSubmiRequisitionPopup(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/UndoSubmitRequisitionPopup",
            data: { prId: '0' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    var navigationID = 0;
                    if(PRMyRequisitionDataView != null &amp;&amp; PRMyRequisitionDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; PRMyRequisitionDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }

                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
                        navigationID = '0';
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                    }

                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnWithdrawMyPR__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {

    function WithdrawRequisitionPopup(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/WithdrawRequisition",
            data: { prId: '0' },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {
                    if(PRMyRequisitionDataView != null &amp;&amp; PRMyRequisitionDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; PRMyRequisitionDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : '0', origin:'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $('#btnApprove__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = '';

        if (prStatus != 'S') {
            ShowAjaxMessage('The requisition should be in submitted status to approve / disapprove.', "error","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove(e);
    });

    function ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove(e) {

        var data = { prId: '0' };

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove",
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    if (result.Success == false) {
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : '', origin:'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '', ValidateRequisitionBeforeApprove: true },type:"POST"});
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "Approve");
                    }

                }
            }
        });
    }

    function ApproveRequisitionOnPopup(e) {
        var approverId = '';

        var selectedRowIds = '';
        var arr = selectedRowIds.split('~');

        var data = { approverId: approverId, approvalTrackingId: selectedRowIds, approvalType: '3' };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            type: "POST",
            async: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/RequisitionApproval/SingleRequisitionApproveAction",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == 1) {
                    var navigationID = 0;

                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
                        closRequisitionActiveWindow(e);
                        ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition approved successfully.', "success");
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function closRequisitionActiveWindow(e) {
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
    }

    function DisapproveRequisitionOnPopup(e) {
        var approverId = '';

        var selectedRowIds = '';

        var data, options;

        data = { approverId: approverId, requireMyAttention: false, approvalTrackingId: selectedRowIds, approvalType: '3' , Ismultiple: false };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/Purchasing/RequisitionApproval/DisapproveRequisition", data: data, type: "POST" };

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowDisapproveRequisition")
       .SetIsModal(true)
       .SetContent(options)
       .SetonClose(function () {
           if ($('#IsDisapprovedProcessed').val() == 1)
           {
               SaveBeforeAnyOperation(e, "Disapprove")
           }
       })
       .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
       .SetTitle('Disapprove Requisition')
       .SetWidth(550)
       .SetHeight(150)
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "RequisitionApproval", null);

    }

    function RefreshPopupAfterDisapproveRequisition(e) {

        var navigationID = 0;

        if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__PurchaseRequisitionView').is(":visible")){
            closRequisitionActiveWindow(e);
            ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition Disapproved successfully.', "success");
        }
        else{
            navigationID = '';
            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'PRMyRequisitionDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/Purchasing/MyPurchaseRequisition/EditMyRequisitionPopup",data: {id : navigationID, origin:'MY_PURCHASE_REQUISITION' , aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, statusType: '3', adminPRApproverId: '' },type:"POST"});
            ShowAjaxMessage('Purchase Requisition Disapproved successfully.', "success","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            UnRegisterActiveScreen();
        }

    }

    $('#btnDisapprove__PurchaseRequisitionView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");

        var prStatus = '';

        if (prStatus != 'S') {
            ShowAjaxMessage('The requisition should be in submitted status to approve / disapprove.', "error","PurchaseRequisitionDetailPopup_Error");
            return;
        }

        DisapproveRequisitionOnPopup(e);
    });

<script>
    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }

    })
